Local News

Yesterday, Various Circles Held a Public Memorial Service for the Late President Tan 87

More than a Thousand People Attended

Yesterday, various circles in this city held a national funeral ceremony for the late President Tan. The Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters specially set up a public memorial hall in the main auditorium on the third floor. Yesterday, leaders and party members from various circles in this city went to pay their respects in large numbers. The details are recorded below:

▲ Arrangement of the Memorial Hall: A bamboo cloth banner was hung at the entrance, reading "Shanghai Public Memorial Hall for the National Funeral Ceremony of the Late President Tan." The spirit tablet of the late President Tan was placed in the memorial hall, along with sacrifices such as fresh flowers and fruits. There were many elegiac couplets from various circles. The Shanghai Municipal Executive Committee wrote (For years, he traveled tirelessly for the revolution, rejoicing in the transformation of the world. The golden vase is intact, and his name is marked in history. From afar, we admire the outstanding figure and the abundant spirit of Hengyue. Hundreds of thousands of administrative affairs have been reorganized, lamenting his diligence for the Party and the country, not even eating or sleeping. The great star falls from the sky, how sad the wind and cold moon is! His heroic soul forever weeps at Zhongshan). The Garrison Headquarters wrote (Building a tomb like Qilian, we all look up to the glory and recall the red shadow, sending Hui and leaving a stone room, knowing that joy and sorrow are tied to the common people). Other elegiac couplets from various circles are very touching, so they are omitted here. The memorial oration is also omitted for its length.

▲ People Who Paid Respects: Leaders from various circles who attended included Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, Chen Xizeng, Director of the Public Security Bureau, Wu Kaixian, Member of the Municipal Party Committee, Wang Xiaolai, Member of the City Chamber of Commerce, Zhou Baoli, Representative of the Garrison Headquarters, Wang Xundi, Representative of the Shanghai Local Court, Ying Shi, President of the Second Special District Court, Liang Renjie of the Jiangsu High Court Third Branch, as well as representatives from various agencies, organizations, and schools, no less than one thousand people.

Yesterday's News on Disaster Relief in Various Provinces 88

Two Batches of Disaster Victims from Hubei and Jiangxi Arrived Yesterday

The Shanghai Relief Office for Disaster Victims in Nanshi received reports from the Railway Bureau and China Merchants Bureau at 4 AM yesterday, stating that a large number of refugees had arrived in Shanghai. Therefore, the office immediately dispatched staff and public security police to receive and accommodate them. The details of the arrival and a glimpse of the disaster victims are recorded below:

▲ Jiangshun Arrived in Shanghai: The Jiangshun of the China Merchants Bureau arrived in port yesterday morning, carrying more than 120 disaster victims from Heyang and Hankou in Hubei. At about 9 AM, they were received and guided to the Liuying Road shelter in Zhabei by the office. Most of them had sunken eyes and tattered clothes. They were mostly villagers from the neighboring counties of Wuhan who relied on farming for a living. It was heard that they had not been frozen or starved on the ship. The comprador on the ship had cooked more than ten baskets of rice and distributed it to the disaster victims.

▲ Train Carried Another Batch of Disaster Victims: Another batch of disaster victims, about sixty from Fengyang, Anhui, were carried by train from Nanjing by the Railway Bureau. Because there were too many disaster victims from Jiangxi, Hubei, Shandong, and Anhui being accommodated in various places in Nanjing, there was almost no room left. Shanghai was specially ordered to receive them. They carried children and luggage, and their situation was quite tragic. They originally wanted to take the same train to Hangzhou to take refuge. However, when the train arrived, two girls, Chen Dadaizi and Chen Xiaodaizi, were lost at the station, so they got off the train to look for them. Later, they were guided to the corner of Xiaoximen by the police, where passers-by distributed relief rations of steamed buns. It was said that they planned to take a train to Hangzhou at the South Station, but the two missing children had not yet been found.

Municipal Party Committee Pays Attention to Disaster Relief 89

The Municipal Executive Committee, in order to raise public awareness of the need for urgent relief for the flood disaster, will invite Mr. Zhu Qinglan to give a lecture next Monday during the memorial week. It has already instructed the party committees of various districts to be informed. The original text is recorded below: (To Order Compliance: This committee, in order to raise public awareness of the need for urgent relief for the flood disaster, has specially designated the memorial week to be held at 9 AM next Monday in the auditorium of our party headquarters. Please invite Mr. Zhu Qinglan to give a lecture. The district party committees are hereby instructed to comply immediately and inform their subordinates, sending four representatives each to attend the meeting. This order.)

Urgent Relief Association Propaganda Group 90

Proposes (Outline of Disaster Relief Propaganda Week Plan)

The Propaganda Group of the All-Provinces Flood Disaster Urgent Relief Association held its third regular meeting on the day before yesterday (3rd) at noon at the Jue Lin Temple. Zhang Zhuping, Wang Boqi, Pan Gongbi, Zhu Xiangxin, Zheng Yaonan, Liu Jinchuan, Zhou Kaijia, Jiang Qudan, Ren Jinping, Jin Xiongbai, Xu Xinyi, Zhu Zunyu, Sun Menghua, Zhang Zhihan, Sun Zhixiang, Sun Choucheng, Chen Binhe, and other seventeen people attended. They unanimously elected Mr. Wang Boqi as chairman to discuss the proposal for the outline of the disaster relief propaganda week. Ren Jinping explained that in order to widely publicize the disaster situation and raise a large amount of relief funds in a short period of time to benefit the disaster victims, the two standing committees of the design group specially drafted an outline for the disaster relief propaganda week and requested everyone to discuss it. After reading and revising each item, it was approved and decided to submit it to the Urgent Relief Association today. After the general meeting approves it, it will be implemented on a scheduled basis. The outline of the disaster relief propaganda week is recorded as follows:

Shanghai Fundraising for All-Provinces Flood Disaster Urgent Relief Association's 91

Disaster Relief Propaganda Week Plan Outline (1) Name: Disaster Relief Propaganda Week; (2) Purpose: To exert one week's effort to achieve widespread publicity and raise 5 million relief funds; (3) Organization: To be organized separately by uniting all public and private organizations, businesses, and individuals in Shanghai; (4) Fundraising: Fundraising matters will be presided over by the Fundraising Group of this Association, and the classification rules are as follows: (1) Relief Plaques: Made of lead, divided into red and blue. Red: one yuan per piece; Blue: two jiao per piece (suitable for both large and small foreign currencies). Every household must purchase and nail one plaque, red or blue, according to their willingness; (2) Relief Badges: Made of lead, divided into red and blue. Red: one yuan per piece; Blue: two jiao per piece (suitable for both large and small foreign currencies). Everyone must purchase and wear one badge, red or blue, according to their willingness; (3) Relief Flags: Cloth flags, divided into red characters and blue characters. Red characters: one yuan per flag; Blue characters: two jiao per flag. Each vehicle must purchase and insert one flag, red or blue, according to their willingness. Business vehicles are purchased by the car companies (suitable for both large and small foreign currencies); (4) Fundraising Teams: Each team has a minimum target of 100 yuan, and more donations are welcome; (5) Special Donations: Entertainment, sports, business, and other special disaster relief activities are all included; (5) Publicity: Publicity matters will be presided over by the Publicity Group of this Association, and the classification rules are as follows: (1) Speeches: (A) Radio Broadcasting; (B) Theaters; (C) Amusement Parks; (D) Public Assembly Halls; (2) Written Materials: (A) Newspapers; (B) Publications, Commentaries, Literature and Art, Illustrations, Slogans, Photos, News; (C) Leaflets; (D) Theater Programs, Slogans; (E) White Cloth Banners on Roads; (3) Advertisements: (A) Newspaper Advertisements; (B) Outdoor Advertisements; (C) Movie Advertisements, Lantern Slide Advertisements (already prepared); (4) Entertainment: (A) Holding Entertainment Events; (B) Arranging Plays; (C) Interludes; (6) Finance: Financial matters, except for the expenses of the Publicity Group, which are borne by itself, are presided over by the Finance Group of this Association, and the classification rules are as follows: (1) Income from Donations; (2) Expenditure of Expenses; (7) Affairs: All affairs not belonging to the Fundraising, Publicity, and Finance Groups are generally presided over by the General Affairs Group of this Association, and the classification rules are as follows: (1) Contacting; (2) Liaison; (3) Distribution; (4) Investigation; (5) Management; (6) Reporting; (7) Statistics; (8) Dates: Propaganda Week is set for one week, and team fundraising is set for one month, with collections and announcements every seven days; (A) Methods for Relief Plaques and Relief Badges: (1) Relief Plaques: Please have the Citizens' Federation of Shanghai handle it by district. The handling methods are divided into two types: (A) Three days before the Disaster Relief Propaganda Week, distribute them to stores near each alley for consignment sales, and this Association will publish an announcement in the newspaper; (B) Starting from the day of the Disaster Relief Propaganda Week, each store will send one clerk to persuade residents and stores that have not purchased or nailed them to purchase them; (2) Relief Badges and Relief Plaques: In addition to entrusting stores to sell them, please ask the Shanghai Education Community Flood Disaster Fundraising Federation and the Chinese Boy Scouts Federation to ask students and Boy Scouts from various schools to persuade people to purchase them along the way in different districts and roads. Female students will persuade households to purchase them (the Shanghai Education Community Flood Disaster Relief Federation has agreed). The dates are tentatively set for Saturday and Sunday, and may be extended if necessary; (B) Methods for Relief Flags: (1) Handle according to the methods for Relief Plaques and Relief Badges; (2) For those who have not purchased or inserted Relief Flags, fundraising teams along the way will persuade them to purchase them on the road starting from the day of the Disaster Relief Propaganda Week; (3) Three days before the Disaster Relief Propaganda Week, this Association will send letters to the Public Security Bureau of the Chinese Concession, the French Concession, and the Public Concession, and the Police Department of the工部局, requesting them to notify the police at each post to do their best to protect the Disaster Relief Propaganda Week; (C) Methods for Fundraising Teams: (1) The organization of the Fundraising Team: Each team is set up with one captain and one vice-captain, and there is no fixed number of team members. Consultants, secretaries, and honorary staff may also be set up, which will be determined by each captain; (2) The Fundraising Team will proceed in the same way as the 微求 Association, but only a report form will be issued, and no other printed materials will be issued. Receipts will be exchanged at the designated collection point; (3) All public and private organizations, trade associations, and labor unions must recognize at least one team, but those who recognize more than ten teams may form a large team; (4) Factories, merchants, and individuals who are willing to organize independently may also join; (5) Detailed regulations will be drafted separately after the decision is made; (D) Classification of Special Donations: (1) All donations that do not belong to the above items are called special donations; (1) Those belonging to entertainment: (A) Dance Halls; (B) Peking Opera Theaters; (C) Movie Theaters; (D) Amusement Parks; (E) Storytelling Theaters; (F) Temporary Entertainment Groups; (2) Those belonging to sports: (A) Sports Meetings; (B) Various Ball Games; (C) Swimming Competitions; (D) Sports Grounds; (E) Swimming Pools; (F) Horse Racing; (3) Those belonging to business: All firms, factories, companies, hotels, restaurants, and shops that engage in business are included; (4) Those belonging to special categories: All special donations that do not belong to the above items are included; (2) This Association will give thank-you certificates to all the above donors; (3) For stores that have donated to disaster relief through business donations before the Disaster Relief Propaganda Week, this Association will give thank-you certificates before the Disaster Relief Propaganda Week; (E) Publicity Methods: (1) The progress of the speech aspect: Draft several kinds of speech reference drafts. The handling methods are divided into two types: (A) Broadcasting and public places will be handled by this group by inviting famous experts; (B) Theaters and amusement parks will be handled by this Association by sending letters to the managers or responsible persons, attaching reference drafts, and asking them to send people or invite people to take charge. Speak once a day, with a time limit of 3 to 5 minutes; (2) The progress of the written aspect: Convene the editors of newspapers and publications, sincerely discuss and determine to do their best uniformly during the Disaster Relief Propaganda Week, or do it by correspondence; (3) Advertisements have been sent to various advertising companies and companies and firms to donate advertising space; (4) Entertainment, drama, and interludes will be done by correspondence.

Telegrams from the Jiangsu Flood Disaster Relief Association 92

(1) Telegram from Baoying: To Chairman Zhu Zhen of the State Council Relief Association Working Group, Chairman Xu, Standing Committee of the Urgent Relief Association Yu Wang Wu, and Chairman Wang Huang of the Jiangsu Relief Association: Baoying is flooded again, the water is rising violently, and the embankment has collapsed for many years. All the weirs in the northeastern countryside have been broken. The number of deaths is difficult to estimate. The city is fortunately safe. The original post office refugee shelter has been renamed refugee shelter, and efforts are being made to send boats to rescue people. Please quickly transport rice and flour to the town. Respectfully, Jingsheng. East. (2) Telegram from Zhenjiang: To Mr. Yilao of the Renji Hall Jiangsu Relief Association: I, De Sui Yiqing, arrived in Zhenjiang late. Yan is escorting a wheel to You to rescue disaster victims. Saw the breach in the east embankment of the Shaobo Great King Temple, and more than half of the entire town was washed away. Several breaches in the Zhaoguan Dam. Arrived in You in the afternoon and found four breaches at Yuma Pier and Dangjunlou. Although the danger to Youcheng has passed, the autumn flood is worrying. A batch of refugees was transported to Yang, and four villages were rescued. Respectfully, Jin Shude, winter. (3) Telegram from Yangzhou: To Mr. Yilao Han of the Jiangsu Flood Disaster Relief Association: I have received your telegram. The disaster situation in the Shaobo rural area, which is located in a remote area, is particularly serious. The tragic state is unbearable to witness. Those who come to seek assistance are constantly coming. The urgent relief is as urgent as a shooting star. Your telegram requested 10,000 yuan, which is far from enough. Please allocate another 10,000 yuan, totaling 20,000 yuan, and allocate 3,000 bags of flour. Please remit and transport them quickly. Looking forward to your reply. Respectfully, Cao Yueshen, Yuan Jimei, winter. (4) Telegram from Yangzhou: To Chairman Song Ziwen of the Flood Relief Committee, Chairman Xu Jingren of the Relief Affairs Committee, the Presidium of the All-Provinces Flood Disaster Urgent Relief Association, and the Jiangsu Flood Disaster Relief Association: Zhi Jiang and I, Shichen, took boats and dry food to inspect the disaster-stricken areas in person and provide urgent relief. I sent a telegram from Yan Shu to your attention. This afternoon, I returned to the office from the disaster areas of Shaobo and Gaoyou. I witnessed the breaches in the river embankment. There are four breaches in Shaobo, totaling about 170 zhang: 20 zhang at the Gongdian, 60 zhang at the Yumatou, 50 zhang at the Hehuatang, 90 zhang at the Dangjunlou, and 60 zhang at the Yumatou. The water rushes straight in, and the current is extremely turbulent. The angry waves roar wildly, and boats cannot get close. The upstream and downstream are a vast expanse of water, almost like the sea, pouring down thousands of miles, beyond the reach of the eye. There are occasional high mounds that are slightly exposed, like isolated islands in the ocean, appearing and disappearing in the vast smoke and waves, which are impossible to reach. After the water passes, houses are flooded and collapse, and deaths under the belly of fish are often heard. The loss of life and property is difficult to count. This is the situation in the Gaoyou area. As for Xinghua and other counties, which are located at the bottom of the pot, transportation is cut off, and special personnel have been sent to visit them. There is still no news. The tragic situation is extremely painful. Now the surviving people have no home to return to, and they are cramped in the wilderness, shivering in the autumn wind. The refugees are difficult to describe. I am ashamed that I do not have Zheng Xia's map. I frequently call out to Jiang Bo and imitate the tongue of Guang Chang. I humbly ask for early compassion and swift relief, coming from a source and the more the better. I cannot help but bow to the disaster victims nine times. Respectfully, Zhang Zhijiang, east. (5) Telegram from Liuzhuang: To the Jiangsu Flood Disaster Relief Association: After the Yun Dam was released, the Yun Embankment continued to collapse. The flood arrived violently, and the water level rose several feet sharply on Yan night. In the winter, the fierce wind and rain caused the water to increase continuously. All the weirs were flooded, the fields and crops were submerged, the houses were washed down, and the people drowned. Now a temporary life-saving association has been formed, and refugee shelters have been set up to temporarily relieve the immediate emergency. I earnestly request the association to send personnel to investigate and provide urgent relief as soon as possible. It is a matter of life and death. Respectfully, the Liuzhuang Flood Disaster Temporary Life-Saving Association, Jiang. (6) To the Jiangsu Flood Disaster Relief Association: We have just received reports from various counties that Xinghua and Dongtai are completely submerged in the province, the entire village of Yancheng is flooded, and the water in Taixian has reached the edge of the city. Disaster victims are gathered everywhere. The Yun Embankment in Taizhou has more than a dozen breaches, and the water is still pouring down. Officials are celebrating the reduction of water in You and Shao, but they do not know that the reduction of water upstream is the subsidence of land downstream. Colleagues are shouting until they are exhausted, and they want to cry without tears. We once again earnestly request all parties to unanimously advocate for awakening the authorities, blocking the breaches as quickly as possible, and raising funds for relief and saving lives together. It is extremely urgent. Respectfully, the Salt Yufu Tai Dong Xing Flood Disaster Relief Association stationed in the town, east. (7) Telegram from Xiaoxian: To the Jiangsu Provincial Relief Association: Since the summer of this year, Xiaoxian has suffered repeated torrential rains and floods. The water in the city is four to five feet deep, and boats are needed to enter the market. All areas are in a huge flood, and the autumn crops have been completely submerged. Many livestock drowned. Special personnel have been sent to various areas to investigate. According to statistics, 1,383 villages have been flooded, more than 17,000 hectares of fields and crops have been flooded, 12,980 houses have collapsed, losses are more than 10 million yuan, and 90,000 people have been affected. 25 people drowned. The disaster situation is extremely serious and there are too many disaster victims. I implore your association to send personnel to the county for investigation as soon as possible, allocate a large amount of money, and provide urgent relief to prevent the old and weak from dying in the ditches and the young and strong from taking risks. I am extremely grateful. (8) Letter from the Jianghuai Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai: Received a telegram from County Magistrate Du of Yancheng: Yanyi is located downstream, and the Yun Embankment has collapsed. The fields are one zhang or seven or eight feet deep. The young and strong are climbing trees to wait for rescue, and most of the women and children have drowned. The houses have been destroyed, and the cooking has been cut off. The tragic situation is unbearable to speak of.

The Xinghua Fellow Villagers Association believes that the water disaster in their hometown is extremely serious, and telegrams are no longer working. Fellow villagers in Shanghai are very concerned, but they do not know the true situation. The association specially sent personnel to return to their hometown to inspect. They departed the night before and sent a letter from Zhen yesterday, saying that they had read a telegram from Xingdai at a friend's place in Zhen, which said (arrived in Xing at noon, the water level along the way is still rising, and there is no dry land in the entire area. Disaster victims are gathered, and there is a shortage of rice and grain. Li Junjun went to Yang and the money has not arrived and is in Li's hand. Mao You River is open and is now being strongly blocked by Dafeng Yuhua. Another telegram was sent to the province to petition. Specially heard.) This telegram was sent from Xing by a special person to Taixian and then forwarded to Zhenjiang.

The Origin of the Taicang Fellow Villagers Association's Request for Relief 94

The Taicang Fellow Villagers Association issued a request for relief yesterday, saying that Heaven does not pity us, and floods are causing disasters. Various provinces have reported emergencies one after another, and Taicang is also suffering from this disaster. Taicang County is located on the east coast of the sea and the west end of Tai Lake. It is known as the land of water. The western countryside is shaped like the bottom of a pot. Once there is more rain, the harvest will be reduced. Therefore, the residents there rarely have savings, and the cry for assistance is often heard. Since the beginning of summer this year, there have been continuous rains, and the western water has been heavy. The fields and crops have been

Page 14

submerged, and the houses have been washed away. Not only is there no harvest, but the clothes, food, and housing are all lacking. The sight of people crying for food and sleeping in the open is everywhere. After on-site investigation, the first, sixth, and eighth districts of the county, namely the old Huchuan, Shuangfeng, Mao市,　叶, Xinfeng, and Zhitang townships, have suffered the most. The disaster of this scale has never happened before. The disaster-stricken fields and crops have reached more than 100,000 mu, and most of them have no harvest. The disaster-stricken houses have reached hundreds of families, and they have all been displaced. On August 25th, the coastal area was hit by a storm surge, which destroyed more than 500 zhang of the sea embankment. Dozens of nearby residents were also destroyed, and the disaster situation is the same. Since the incident, the local government has organized a flood disaster relief committee, but the disaster situation is very serious, and I am deeply afraid that it is just a drop in the bucket. We rely entirely on raising funds from various sources to provide rescue. The fellow villagers are concerned about their hometown and cannot ignore the situation. After a meeting and discussion, in addition to considering the funds at the scene, we believe that gathering strength can achieve success, and accumulating sand can make a tower. I implore all kind people from all walks of life to generously donate and help as much as they can. A thousand taels is not too much, and one wen is not too little. A few more wen can save one more life, and saving one day means fewer people will die. This can inspire heaven and earth and save the catastrophe. The merits and virtues are limitless. We respectfully bow to all the disaster victims in the county nine times and ask for your urgent words. Please be aware of this. Shanghai Taicang Fellow Villagers Association Executive Committee Xiang Huiqing, Hu Cuishi, Zhang Bianxiang, Wang Boxun, Zhu Kai　, Jin Xiawen, Fu Zayan, Xiang Huaqing, Hong Jingping, Wu Zhongbao, Hu Yuanming, Lu Jingshi, Yu Tingwu, Wang Jizhang, Wang Tianjue, Zhou Kuanfu, Xiang Ganbo, Wu Jingwen, Gu Zorong, Jin Yunzhong, Ye Zhengong, and others. It is also learned that this matter was initiated by Mr. Tang Weizhi and others. The association collected 1,000 yuan yesterday. The Shanghai Jisheng Association also allocated 3,000 yuan to the Taicang branch for preliminary relief.

The Shanghai Special Zone Citizens' Federation's Flood Disaster Relief Appeal Team, after yesterday's committee meeting, decided to divide into teams and set off for marches on various roads, starting from September 6th for a total of five days (postponed in case of rain). Anhui Fellow Villagers Host the Press 96

The Anhui Flood Disaster Relief Association in Shanghai, because the disaster situation in Anhui Province is particularly serious, even more tragic than in Jiangsu and Hubei, invited the Shanghai press to the New New Restaurant at 3 pm yesterday, including Zhang Zhuping, Wang Boqi, Wang Yingbin, Yu Kongwo, Yuan Yeyu, etc. Xu Shiying, Guan Yunnong, Xu Jingren, Yu Langxi, Wang Baozhai, and other ten members of the Standing Committee of the association hosted everything. First, Chairman Xu Shiying reported the disaster situation in 48 counties in Anhui Province. Due to traffic congestion and undeveloped people, there is a lack of propaganda. I hope that the press will provide more guidance so that the disaster victims in each county can be rescued earlier. Guan Yunnong said, (1) This association is very cautious about disaster relief and fundraising. All donations received will be used for disaster relief. The association's affairs and entertainment expenses are all recognized by colleagues. (2) The release of relief funds will be assigned to familiar with disaster relief and impartial personnel designated by the association to distribute in the disaster areas, without any handling to avoid abuses. Liu Lian in northern Anhui, Xu Pinxian in central Anhui, and Wu Songting in southern Anhui, etc. It is also hoped that all sectors will supervise at any time so that the disaster victims will benefit without any bias. Finally, Zhang Zhuping gave a reply on behalf of the association, and the meeting adjourned at 5 pm.

Recent Disaster Situation in Various Counties in Anhui 97

This national flood has particularly affected Anhui Province. The following is a summary of the disaster reports received by the Anhui Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai, the All-Provinces Flood Disaster Urgent Relief Association, etc.

▲On the 14th of last month, the Huangsitan Dam in Wuwei collapsed. All 940 large and small weirs in the county were submerged. Countless people, livestock, and houses were washed away. Corpses swelled, decayed, and smelled unbearably like ducks. Until now, the wind and waves are still shaking. The 260-mile single embankment along the river is fighting for life with the water. If it is not repaired, it will become a permanent giant mooring, which is related to the seven counties of Lu and He. According to statistics, 121,400 households and 746,770 people were affected in the nine districts of the county. 350,720 people are homeless, and 416,270 people are in urgent need of relief. 1,496,070 mu of farmland have been flooded. The harvest in the first, fourth, fifth, and third districts this year is completely hopeless. In other districts, at most, only 1% can be harvested.

▲In Chaoxian, there were continuous heavy rains for six or seven days last month, and the lake water rose sharply by two zhang. A total of 166 weirs in the entire territory, totaling more than 360,000 mu of fields, the dikes collapsed, and the fields and crops were submerged. The water in the city was several feet deep.

▲In Xuancheng, all 200 weirs in the county collapsed completely. Taking Xihe Town as an example, more than 50 houses were washed away, and more than 1,000 people drowned. Party and government agencies raised more than 6,000 yuan to provide temporary relief, which is far from enough. In addition, the Xihe Shenggong Weir, Luogong Weir, Wancun Weir, Baoxing Weir, and other hundreds of miles are a vast expanse of water, and the disaster is particularly serious.

▲In Jixi, after heavy rain last month, it was hit by a strong wind on the 26th, followed by hail. The water was more than eight feet high, and people and animals were drowned.

▲In Xiuning, there was heavy rain from the 18th of last month. The water was one zhang high in low-lying areas. People could not escape, climbed on the roof and shouted for help. The walls collapsed, and the grain was empty. The disaster-stricken villages reached more than 80, more than 2,000 mu of fields were flooded, and hundreds of houses collapsed.

News from the Red Cross Society on Disaster Relief 98

▲Overseas Chinese from the Bandit Island Donate Rice for Relief: The Chinese Red Cross Society in this port received a telegram from Mr. Yang, an overseas Chinese from the Philippines, saying that he had personally donated 500 bags of rice and sent them to the National Government Disaster Relief Committee, asking them to designate the Red Cross Society to distribute them. At the same time, his representative in Shanghai, Mr. Yang Mengchu, went to the Red Cross Society to discuss everything.

▲Meifu Foreign Firm Saves Meals to Help Relief: Employees of the Meifu Foreign Firm have always held meal gatherings. This month, because the water disaster is particularly serious, they specially saved the meal fees and donated them to the Red Cross Society.

Disaster Relief Work of the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association 99

▲Telegram urging Priest Rao to go to Yang: Priest Qian Jiaju, the western president of the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association, set off for Hankou last month to handle urgent relief matters. Now, the flood disaster in Jiangbei is even more serious than in Wuhan. Vice President Gu Jisheng and others of the association have already set off for Yang, but the disaster area is relatively wide. Therefore, the association telegraphed Han yesterday, urging Priest Rao to transfer to Yangzhou to handle urgent relief in Jiangbei.

▲Setting up donation boxes for flood disasters: The association recently prepared many donation boxes for flood disasters and sent them to Shui'an, Xianshi, and Xinxin yesterday, set up in appropriate places to make customers feel shocked and happy to donate, accumulating sand to form a tower, and should be able to save many disaster victims.

▲Overseas Chinese generously donate large sums: Yesterday, the association received several donations remitted by overseas Chinese: (1) Guangdong Bank in New York remitted donations from three overseas Chinese, Yuan, Wu, and Chen, one for 1,150 yuan, one for 3,000 yuan, and one for 3,040 yuan; (2) Citizens of Honolulu remitted 11,000 yuan for relief; (3) The Ontario Overseas Chinese Flood Disaster Relief Association in Canada remitted 5,000 foreign yuan. Those who donate in this port are also coming in an endless stream.

▲Report from the Taizhou Branch: Yesterday, the association received a letter from the Taizhou Branch reporting that the situation in Taizhou is very bad. Disaster victims from Dongtai, Xinghua, Yancheng, and other places have fled to Taizhou City. There are now more than 80,000 disaster victims in the city waiting to be fed. The Taizhou Branch has found ways to provide relief. In addition, Qingjiangpu and Huai'an have also begun to organize branches to handle urgent relief matters.

News from the French Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association 100

▲Soliciting clothes and quilts: According to the office of the French Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association, which was established to solicit clothes and quilts for disaster victims, it has already started working. In recent days, citizens from all walks of life have enthusiastically donated all their cotton clothes and quilts.

▲The Superintendent of the French Concession, Fevrier, replies in a direct reply: Received a letter stating that the flood disaster in various provinces is extremely serious and that relief should not be delayed. Therefore, he convened a meeting of the executive supervisors on the 31st of last month to organize a disaster relief committee, and decided to produce pictures of disaster victims and various fundraising texts for posting and distribution within the concession. Please inform all police stations that in the event of posting and distributing the above pictures and texts, please do not misunderstand. Also, please transfer to the advertising tax office to exempt advertising tax, etc. After investigation, the pictures of disaster victims and fundraising texts are related to good deeds and are allowed to be posted and distributed within the concession. However, more than ten copies of each of these pictures and texts must be sent to this office for redistribution to the police stations as sample sheets. Those that should be posted must be sent to the advertising tax office of this office for free stamping. Correspondingly reply, I hope you will investigate and deal with it accordingly. Best regards to the French Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association, Fevrier, stamped, September 3rd.

A Refugee Hospital Ship Organized by Foreigners Will Go to Han 101

The disaster relief committee organized by foreigners in this port chartered the Hannan Moller of the Moller Company as a refugee hospital ship for sick refugees after a meeting on the afternoon of the 3rd. The ship was scheduled to sail into the Jiangnan Shipyard for conversion yesterday morning. Once the work is completed, it plans to rush to Hankou. The ship has a deadweight of 3,300 tons and can accommodate between 150 and 200 sickbeds. In addition, there are 10 small rooms and one large dining room, which can be used by police officers. Renji Hospital has agreed to send three doctors to serve on the ship, with Dr. Robert Benson as the director, assisted by Dr. Thomson and Dr. Maxswell. Or two health inspectors will be sent to handle cleaning and prevent infectious diseases. After the ship arrives in Han, it will cooperate with the medical staff in the port to carry out everything. The local Kehua Pharmacy has donated 3,000 taels of silver for the purchase of medicines. However, this move requires a lot of money, and I hope that philanthropists will contribute to the good cause. The conversion project of the ship can be completed in about five or six days. Then it will be loaded with coal and rush to Han. The 400 tons of coal needed has been recognized by the Kailuan Coal Mine Company.

Mao Heyuan Discusses the Ning Shao Relief Team's Journey to Wuhan 102

The Ning Shao fellow villagers' emergency relief association for the Wuhan disaster sent the Xin Ning and Yong Xing steamers to Wuhan to carry fellow villagers for assistance. Both ships have arrived in Ningbo one after another. All members of the relief team sent by the association to Wuhan returned to Shanghai on the first of this month. Yesterday, our reporter interviewed Mr. Mao Heyuan, the director of the team, at the Ningbo fellow villagers association, who made the following statement. The reporter asked, "We heard that the Xin Ning and Yong Xing steamers were not crowded with fellow villagers on their way down from Wuhan. What was the reason for this?" Mr. Mao replied, "There were two trips for fellow villagers returning to their hometowns, totaling about 1,500 people. The reason is that after the 23rd, the floodwaters receded day by day, and people's hearts gradually settled down. Most fellow villagers were unwilling to leave Wuhan easily due to property and job concerns, so the ships were not very crowded. " The reporter also asked, "It seems that fellow villagers in Shanghai have some criticisms of the gentlemen who went to Wuhan. Have you heard of this?" Mr. Mao replied, "I heard about it as soon as I arrived in Shanghai, but the facts are all there, and I think the rumors will soon subside. Mr. Xie Qigang and Mr. Hong Xuefan and I usually pay attention to personal hygiene. When we took the Longhe ship to Wuhan, we sat in the first-class cabin, but the cabin fare and liquor expenses were all paid by ourselves. As for the drinking water and food we brought, we couldn't prepare much at the beginning because the Hua Wu ship had no facilities, so some of it can still be returned. The expenses were also paid by ourselves, without using public funds. Compared to the charitable leaders of various charitable organizations who practice frugality and self-discipline, I am indeed far inferior. However, I dare to ask myself that I did not waste public funds, and I believe that fellow villagers will understand. The round trip took a total of eleven days and cost more than 2,100 yuan, and I have instructed Mr. Chen, the accountant of our team, to prepare a detailed report," he said.

Tang Hai'an, the superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, personally went to various Chinese and foreign companies to solicit donations. He has now raised 110,000 yuan, all of which have been issued by Tang to the National Government Flood Relief Committee for receipts to show credibility.

Yesterday, the Book Industry Association convened a meeting of all members to solicit donations. As a result, on-the-spot pledges amounted to 7,500 yuan.

▲ Donation Method for the Shipping Industry

Yesterday, the shipping industry in this city discussed ways to provide disaster relief. After detailed discussion at a meeting of the trade association, the following methods were decided: (1) Notify all companies to deduct 10% from the salaries of employees at all levels. (2) After the company collects donations from employees, the company will double the donation. (3) Within ten days, the donations will be sent to the shipping association for transfer to the disaster relief organization.

German Cargo Ship Hits a Reef 104

The Pachenland Ship

Runs Aground Due to Fog

Yesterday, there was fog on the sea. The cargo ship of the German company Xiangbao in this port, while sailing from Japan to Shanghai, encountered fog and hit a reef. The Shanghai office is already trying to rescue the ship. The information obtained is reported as follows:

▲ Location of the Grounding

The German company Xiangbao's cargo ship, the Pachenland, is a newly built Sino-German liner with a deadweight of 9,000 tons. The engine uses a new type of motorcycle engine and is dedicated to the Xiangbao Shanghai route. This time, the ship came to Shanghai from Germany. After unloading the goods, it went to Japan, and then went to North China to transport soybeans and other miscellaneous grains to Shanghai. It was scheduled to export from Shanghai on the 11th. However, the ship sailed out of Kobe, Japan, and at 3:05 pm yesterday, it arrived at 126 degrees 10 minutes east longitude and 34 degrees 04 minutes north latitude, near Pokusa Island. The ship planned to temporarily stop to avoid the fog, but it had already deviated from the channel, and the hull collided with a reef near the island, damaging the bottom of the ship.

▲ Ship Owner's Report

After the ship accident, the ship owner, Mr. Diniq, reported that the hull had hit a reef, the bottom of the ship was broken, and seawater had entered the cabin. The ship owner urgently sent a wireless SOS signal. The Wu Song Coast Radio Station of the Ministry of Transportation accepted the message and immediately transferred it to the Hengbao Company on Guangdong Road. The company sent a telegram to inquire about the cause of the accident and the extent of the damage. At about 6:00, the ship owner's reply arrived. The manager of the company personally translated and read it, and immediately discussed the rescue.

▲ Sending a Ship for Rescue

After the news of the ship accident reached Shanghai, the manager of Hengbao Shipping Company was still discussing the matter in the company late at night and decided to send a ship to the site for rescue. It is said that the company plans to ask Huidefeng in this port to first send a large tugboat to the location of the Pachenland accident to try to tow it. They will also send personnel to inspect the damage to facilitate repairs and fill the holes, and then tow it. The export date of the ship has already been postponed.

News of the Zhaoxing Ship Accident Rescue 105

All Crew and Passengers Are Safe

▲ Repairs in Shanghai

The Zhaoxing ship of the Zhaoxing Company in this port, which originally operated on the Yangtze River route, stopped in Lushun for ship repairs due to the shortage of goods in Wuhan caused by the flood. The entire repair has now been completed. It loaded soybeans, miscellaneous goods, and passengers in Yingkou and sailed to Shanghai on the 1st. On the afternoon of the 2nd, when the ship arrived at Qingshan Head on the Shandong Sea, the ship received a weather telegram stating that a hurricane would occur on the sea. The ship's captain, Zhang Jidan, in order to prevent harm, ordered the ship to sail to Shidao Bay to avoid the wind. Unexpectedly, before entering the bay, it ran aground on a reef.

▲ The Truth About the Grounding

On the evening of the 2nd, the Zhaoxing ship sailed to Shidao and was about to enter the sea to drop anchor to avoid the wind. Unexpectedly, it ran aground on a reef outside Shidao Bay. The bow cabin of the Zhaoxing ship was pierced by the reef, and seawater rushed into the bow cabin.

The ship's captain, Zhang Jidan, sent a telegram for help. Considering that the ship was aground on the reef and the hull was very dangerous, and deeply worried that seawater would flood the cabins, which would cause the ship to sink, he immediately reversed and ventured to drive the ship onto a nearby beach, so that the hull was aground on the beach to avoid the danger of sinking. Yesterday, a telegram was received stating that the ship was safer in the shallow sand on the coast.

▲ Sending Ships to Help

After receiving the report, the company sent a telegram to Yingkou yesterday, ordering the Huyu liner Hexing, which is currently sailing, and the Yingkou Yantai liner Rongxing to rush to Qingshan Head Shidao Bay to rescue the Zhaoxing. Yesterday, the Shanghai office continued to receive a telegram stating that the Rongxing ship had arrived in Shidao first and decided to unload the cargo inside the Zhaoxing ship and carry it to Shanghai instead, so that the Zhaoxing could reduce its load. Then, it would repair the broken holes, pump out the accumulated water, and then tow it for rescue. The Hexing ship is expected to arrive there today to assist in the rescue.

▲ Crew and Passengers Are Safe

According to Mr. Chen Ganqing, the general ship owner of the company, who spoke to reporters yesterday, the cargo in the bow cabin of the Zhaoxing ship has been damaged by water and suffered losses, but the passengers and employees on the ship are all safe and sound. The Rongxing has arrived and is expected to transfer the cargo and passengers to Shanghai. Although the Zhaoxing ship ran aground, the crisis has passed and it can be towed to safety. The ship will resume the Yangtze River route after the floodwaters in Hankou recede slightly, he said.

Correcting the Date of Establishment of the Kuomintang 106

To the Tenth Day of the Tenth Month of the Eighth Year

The Chinese Kuomintang has a long history. Since the Xingzhong Society until now, it has undergone several reorganizations, and its name has also changed with the reorganizations. According to the current Chinese Kuomintang, it was reorganized from the Chinese Revolutionary Party. The date of reorganization has now been verified by the Central Committee as the tenth day of the tenth month of the eighth year of the Republic of China, not November of the ninth year of the Republic of China. The Third District Party Department of this city has been ordered to instruct its subordinates to make corrections accordingly.

Overseas Chinese Expelled from the Dutch East Indies Arrive in Shanghai 108

Min Weixin, Huang Jingqun

Min Weixin, a standing committee member of the executive committee of the Kuomintang branch in Xijin, and Mr. Huang Jingqun, the dean of studies at Zhongshan Public School, were both expelled from the country. Mr. Min left Xijin by ship on the 13th of last month and arrived in Shanghai yesterday. Su Xin'an sent multiple telegrams to the Central Party Department, requesting the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate, and specially sent Feng Hanyue to report to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. All telegram drafts and documents for the negotiations were inspected by Wei Xingmin, the Hanwu Division of Yicheng, in early November last year. They were deemed to violate the laws of the Dutch East Indies and were detrimental to public security. After repeated interrogations, Mr. Min was ordered to be monitored by Ding police, fingerprinted, photographed as a prisoner, and his residence permit was confiscated. He was also required to sign in at the police station at a fixed time every day for ten months before being ordered to leave the country on August 13 this year. Mr. Huang was the former principal of Zhongshan Public School. In early November last year, Wei Xingmin, the Hanwu Division of Xijiang, came to Xijin and made many harsh demands on the school's facilities and equipment. In early February this year, when the local government of Xijiang went to investigate textbooks, they took the opportunity to imprison him. Mr. Huang was imprisoned for eight days, wearing yellow clothes, eating yellow rice, and doing coconut shell work every day. In early March, the Xijiang authorities ordered that Mr. Huang be strictly interrogated, and then his residence permit was confiscated, fingerprinted, photographed as a prisoner, and police officers were dispatched to monitor his actions. He was required to sign in at the police station at a fixed time every day for five months before being expelled from the country on August 13.

Minutes of the Shanghai Municipal Council Meeting 111

Plan to Prevent the Spread of Infectious Diseases by Disaster Victims Coming to Shanghai

The Public Concession Shanghai Municipal Council announced the various cases discussed at the board meeting on the 2nd of this month: (1) Announcement of Staff Members of the Publicity Department. A director stated that he had contacted the Daily Newspaper Association regarding the candidates for the Chinese news publicist, and they will be submitted to the Chinese directors soon. Another director stated that the Japanese news publicist candidates are also expected to be launched by the Japanese community soon. (2) Extramural Road Case. The Secretary-General reported that the Shanghai Municipal Government has sent representatives to negotiate this matter with the Bureau, and a preparatory meeting has been held once, and it is expected that consultations will continue soon. (3) Fang Dan Land Micro-Tax Issue. The Chairman proposed to postpone the consideration and discuss it after he and the Secretary-General have consulted. (4) Municipal Funding Allocation Issue. It was decided to ask the Secretary-General and the Director of the Accounting Office to contact and make a proposal, hoping to include a definite number in the 1932 budget, specifically for subsidizing Chinese public welfare organizations. The directors all said that there should be a fixed amount for this type of thing every year, which should be clearly included in the budget. It should not be overspent unless there are special circumstances. (5) Disaster Victim Issue. The Director of the Health Department reported on the plan to prevent the spread of infectious diseases by disaster victims coming to Shanghai, and advocated that the Health Department be allowed to recruit volunteer personnel with nursing experience for temporary use when needed. Subsequently, the Chairman reported on the situation of attending the representative meeting of the local health authorities in this port a few days ago. The association hopes that the shelter will be set up on a small beach in the Pudong area of the Huangpu River, so that it can be isolated from the outside world. For the sake of the health of the residents of the concession, he has agreed to share the construction costs of the shelter after it is approved by the board of directors. The directors decided to notify the relevant authorities that the Bureau would immediately share the expenses after receiving the expenditure report. Regarding the Deputy Chairman's suggestion to establish a deeper traffic isolation zone, the Chairman should ask the initiators of the shelter plan to pay attention to this traffic isolation zone, which should be set up in a place far away from Shanghai, so that disaster victims will not avoid quarantine. Finally, the request of the Western Relief Committee to sell flags to raise donations on the 12th was approved, and the meeting adjourned.

The Disturbance in the French Concession Yesterday 113

Indecent Assault on Women Leads to a Major Fight

Detained Workers Awaiting Interrogation

At about 11:00 am yesterday, a dispute occurred in Shenyuli, Huacheng Road, French Concession, when workers of the French electricity company indecently assaulted women, causing a major fight between the two sides. At about 5:00 pm, the workers gathered again to seek revenge and gathered in front of the Songshan Road Police Station, demanding the release of the detained workers. As a result, the police could not stop them and fired two shots into the sky to disperse them. Seven arrested workers are still being held at the police station awaiting interrogation. The details are recorded as follows:

▲ A'e is Seventeen Years Old

Li Genfa, a native of Ningbo, is 24 years old and has been working in the import department of the Dalai Foreign Company on Guangdong Road in this port. He is extremely loyal. His family is in his hometown. Because he is alone in Shanghai to make a living and lacks care, he brought his sister to Shanghai and rented a room in the four-pavilion room in Shenyuli, No. 4, Lane 45, Huacheng Road, French Concession. His sister's name is A'e, she is seventeen years old, and she has a slightly attractive appearance. However, she is very gentle and assists her brother in cooking and washing all kinds of chores.

▲ Ladder Blocks the Way Home

At about 11:00 am yesterday, the Gao family at No. 5, the left neighbor of Li, installed electricity. The electric company ordered three workers to go to work. At that time, in addition to carrying all the necessary equipment, the workers also carried a long bamboo ladder on their shoulders and placed it in the narrow lane behind No. 5. While they were working, Li's sister A'e happened to return home from buying coal briquettes. When she stepped into the alley, the ladder was blocking the way home.

▲ Workers Make Indecent Jokes

At that time, A'e saw that the ladder was placed across the alley and could not pass, so she negotiated with the workers. Unexpectedly, the workers not only refused, but also made indecent jokes and threw mud on A'e's face. A'e argued with them, and as a result, she was slapped by the workers. A'e was a weak woman and did not dare to resist, so she cried loudly. The neighbors heard the sound and gathered together. Seeing the situation, they all felt injustice and beat the workers without asking the reason.

▲ Li Genfa Was Beaten

At that time, the workers returned to the factory after finishing their work because they were outnumbered. At about 5:00 pm, the beaten workers gathered more than 50 workers and rushed to Huacheng Road. When Li Genfa happened to return home from work, the workers shouted and knocked Li down and beat him. Li's waist was seriously injured, and a raincoat was taken away. At that time, a Western police officer was patrolling and, fearing that it would cause trouble, rushed to the Xiaobeimen Police Station and reported to the Songshan Road Police Station by telephone.

▲ Secretly Following the Workers

After receiving the news, the police station immediately dispatched dozens of reserve teams in cars and rushed to suppress them. When they arrived there, there was no trace of the workers, so they returned to the police station. However, when Li was besieged and beaten, a friend of Li's named Zhuang Zifa happened to witness a worker taking Li's raincoat. Zhuang remained silent and secretly followed the worker, waiting for an opportunity to call the police.

▲ Pointing Out the Attacking Workers

Zhuang followed to the vicinity of the Baxianqiao and saw the worker stepping into the Quan'an Tea House. Zhuang rushed to report to the Songshan Road Police Station. The police chief sent a detective to arrest him. When they arrived at Quan'an, there were Shanghai Municipal Council workers playing mahjong in the building. Zhuang pointed out one of the attacking workers on the spot. The detectives were about to arrest him, but the workers resisted. As a result, Li Hesheng and three others were arrested and taken to the police station together.

▲ Li Genfa Was Beaten Again

Seeing that three people had been arrested, the workers immediately gathered more than a hundred people and went to the Songshan Road Police Station to demand their immediate release. In order to eliminate the trouble, the police station did not pursue the matter deeply and released the three people at any time. Unexpectedly, it happened that while the three people were being released, the beaten Li Genfa was reporting to the police station by car. When the workers saw Li getting off the car, they attacked him again.

▲ Detectives and Police Officers Were Slightly Injured

At that time, the police station also transferred many detectives and police officers to suppress the situation, but the workers were so fierce that they could not be stopped. The detectives and police officers fired two shots into the sky before being forced to retreat. In the chaos at the time, police officers Nos. 675, 340, and 370, as well as Western Detective Chief Barti No. 10, Western Detective No. 61, and a Russian detective were slightly injured. The police chief ordered arrests, and a total of seven people were arrested.

▲ Names of the Seven Arrested

Among the seven arrested, four were workers from the electricity company and three were workers from the Shanghai Municipal Council. The electricity company included Chen A from the Takagi workshop, Zhao Liang from the Fourth Water Department, Yu Jinsheng from the Takagi workshop, and Zhu Along. The Shanghai Municipal Council included Zhao Jinsheng from the Madajian, Chen Baobao, a tile craftsman, and Gao Afu, a blacksmith. They are currently being held at the police station awaiting interrogation by the Second Special Court. The police station has also ordered a large number of detectives and police officers to patrol to prevent further incidents. The tram company immediately entered all vehicles into the factory at 8:10 pm last night.

The Fraudulent "Han Disaster Relief for Cantonese People" Group Cheats Money 114

Broken up at the Great Eastern Hotel

Donations Don't Match Receipts

Advertisements Placed to Recruit Liaison Officers

Guo Biao's Solemn Statement

This month on the 3rd, this newspaper carried an advertisement for recruiting liaison officers, which roughly stated that they were urgently seeking ten liaison officers who must be eloquent and loyal, with no guarantee required, and a daily salary of two yuan. Those willing to apply should come to Room 123 on the second floor of the Great Eastern Hotel between 7 PM and 10 PM tonight (the 3rd), and would not be accepted after that. However, the advertisement was unsigned. Generally, people who considered themselves qualified to apply,

envied the generous salary and simple procedures, and the fact that no guarantee was required. That evening, many people flocked to Room 123 of the Great Eastern Hotel on Nanjing Road to register. However, they were refused admission by the men and women residing in the room, who said that the positions were already filled. Those who arrived later were rejected, leaving the applicants extremely disappointed. They gathered outside the room, lamenting their bad luck. However, people continued to arrive in a steady stream. By 10 PM,

a crowd of sixty or seventy people had gathered, and there was much discussion. Some said that the advertisement was a fraudulent act, while others said that since the people in the room claimed that the positions were filled, they should announce the names of those hired or introduce them, otherwise it would be difficult to return home. In the midst of the commotion, the matter came to the attention of Chinese Detective Chief Wang Yingjie and Western Detective Chief Kang Ying of the Lao Zha Police Station, who immediately led officers to investigate the truth. When the officers arrived, the people in the room pointed to the crowd of applicants as those who were trying to extort them, while the crowd claimed that the men and women were colluding to cheat. Each side had its own version of events. The officers then began to investigate and saw a yellow sign with black characters hanging outside the room, reading

"Han Disaster Relief for Cantonese People," and a green poster with black characters advertising for donations. Upon searching the room, they found a donation book, two receipt books, a bundle of "Hankou Flood Relief" advertisements, eight silk badges, all stamped with the seal of the "Han Disaster Relief for Cantonese People" group, and one seal, as well as a smoking set. However, the amount of donations recorded in the donation book was 447 yuan, while

the receipts only amounted to 41 yuan, a significant discrepancy. When questioned about their names and their mission in Shanghai, the men and women said that the two men were Zheng Youqing (also known as Zheng Boxun) and Lin Shanbo, and the two women were Zheng Wangshi, about 30 years old, and Tang Jinghua, about 20 years old, all from Guangdong. Due to the severe flooding in Wuhan, the suffering of the people was unprecedented. People from various places who were living in Hankou were heartbroken and had organized groups to raise funds for relief. However, the Cantonese community in Hankou had not yet taken such action. As citizens of the country, they could not stand idly by, so they and ten other comrades formed the "Han Disaster Relief for Cantonese People" group, and sent these four to Shanghai on the 27th of last month to solicit donations. After arriving in Shanghai, Zheng Youqing

went to the Guangzhao Public Association to ask for assistance. He met with the directors Guo Biao and Chen Bingqian, who generously donated 6,000 yuan. The association sent Cheng Bingkui with Zheng Youqing to take the money to Hankou for distribution. Later, Zheng was unable to go due to other matters, so Cheng went alone. This matter was reported in the newspapers at the time. The recruitment of liaison officers was a separate matter, as they wanted to establish a

copper cigarette case manufacturing business and were recruiting liaison officers to sell the cigarette cases, not to solicit donations. However, due to the lack of capital and the undecided factory location, manufacturing had not yet begun. When the officers asked about the location of the donated funds and the discrepancy between the donation book and the receipts, Zheng vehemently denied any wrongdoing, saying that the donations in the book were filled out by himself and were meant to encourage donations, and that the actual amount should be based on the receipts. As for the 41 yuan that was donated, he initially said it was used for travel expenses, but then claimed it was deposited at the Juchang pawnshop at 112 Wusong Road. The officers found their words contradictory and their behavior suspicious, so they first took Zheng Youqing to Guo Biao to inquire whether the Guangzhao Public Association had made a donation. Guo stated that Zheng Youqing was not qualified to solicit donations, and that Shanghai

has formal Cantonese organizations and the Guangzhao Public Association handles public welfare matters; others should not interfere. The officers then took Zheng to the Juchang pawnshop on Wusong Road to inquire, and the owner, Zheng Ayuan, said that although Youqing was his son, he did not engage in proper employment and had left Shanghai for Hankou with his concubine three years ago and had not been heard from since. Although he had returned to Shanghai, he had not entered the family home, and he did not respond when called. In reality,

the relationship between father and son was worse than that of strangers, so how could he have funds deposited in the shop? The officers then realized that Zheng's actions were indeed fraudulent, so they took him back to the hotel and arrested the other man and two women and took them to the police station. Zheng still did not repent and claimed that he had not committed any illegal acts and that the officers should not interfere. However, the officers arrested the four men and women along with the items found, and those who had come to apply dispersed. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special District Court, where Judge Cheng Shangfeng opened the court for interrogation. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu, based on Article 363 of the Criminal Code,

brought charges of fraud. Zhu Xiaoliang, Tian Jiucheng, Lu Peilin, and three other men who had gone to apply also appeared as witnesses. The remaining people who had gone to apply, some lived far away, and some did not want to go to court because they had not lost money, so they were not listed. First, lawyer Qian described the occurrence of the case, arguing that the eight silk badges that were found were enough to prove that the people recruited by the defendants were in fact to be used to obtain donations, and that their claim to be preparing to promote goods in the future was not credible. However, this case still needed investigation, and an extension was requested. Then, the Chinese and Western detective chiefs reported the details of the case. Witness Zhu Xiaoliang, the current principal of Chengcai Primary School on Yanhai Road, Lao Beimen

because his younger cousin wanted to apply after seeing the advertisement, so he went to apply on his behalf. Zhu was eloquent and thoroughly explained the defendants' false names and fraudulent content, and revealed everything. Then Judge Cheng interrogated the four defendants in order. Zheng Youqing claimed to live in Changxingli, Ermatou, Hankou, and was dispatched by the Zhen Tuan to come to Shanghai to solicit donations, and his other words were similar to his previous statements. Lin Shanbo claimed to work as a street vendor at Dexing Hardware Store in Hankou. This time, Zheng invited him to come to Shanghai on August 27 to solicit donations. Zheng Wangshi also claimed that Zheng invited her to come. Although Tang Jinghua was from Guangdong, she spoke with a Tianjin accent.

Her demeanor was especially calm, quite like a scholarly figure. She lived next door to Zheng in Hankou. After arriving in Shanghai, she initially lived at a friend's place. She only moved to Great Eastern on the first of this month. Her mission was also said to be to help solicit donations. Judge Cheng then ordered the defendants to each post a bail of 1,000 yuan and adjourned the hearing for seven days.

Haddon's Estate Issue 115

Conflicting Opinions from Haddon's Family

The Will Procedures Are Extremely Complete

There Are No Cousins

The Inheritance Tax Is Still Under Review

After the death of British Jewish tycoon Haddon, his estate was estimated to be between 150 million and 200 million yuan. Recently, his cousin, Yitzhak Abraham Haddon, hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit seeking a share of the estate, which has attracted much attention from society. Yesterday, this newspaper's reporter specifically interviewed a confidant of Haddon's wife to inquire about the truth of the matter. According to him, although this matter has been reported in the newspapers, Haddon's wife has not yet received any formal letter from a lawyer, so it is uncertain whether it is true. As for Haddon's brothers, they are almost all dead, and those who remain are only distant relatives. As for the so-called cousin Yitzhak Haddon, I have been close to Haddon for nearly 25 years and know everything, but I have never known such a person. Haddon's illness began in February of last year, and he was bedridden for more than a year. Not once did this so-called cousin come to inquire. The newspaper reported that Haddon had once given a relief sum of 1,000 yuan, but Haddon's lifetime miscellaneous expenses all had ledgers to prove them, but there was absolutely no such payment. The claim is clearly fabricated. As for the marriage contract, Haddon and Mrs. Carling were married in a Jewish synagogue. When they held their golden wedding anniversary four or five years ago, they registered at the British consulate, so there were no problems in terms of law and religious regulations. Secondly, regarding the will issue, Haddon prepared the will in advance when he was seriously ill this spring. At that time, lawyer Gao Yi and Jewish bishop Ellis were present to witness, and Haddon personally signed it. The legal procedures were extremely complete. Haddon's will consisted of only a few words, roughly stating that his property was to be entirely inherited by his wife, Luo Carling, and after his wife's death, it would be given to his adopted children. Moreover, the so-called cousin Yitzhak Haddon has never directly expressed anything to Mrs. Luo. There is no basis in reason or sentiment, so it can only be laughed off.

Furthermore, Haddon's estate consists of land, houses, and other real estate. The inheritance tax is still under review and investigation. Before it is clearly assessed, the estate cannot be used, so the debts and recent donations have all been borrowed from various sources.

Liang Chengyu Executed 116

Kidnapping for Ransom and Harboring Kidnappers

Liang Chengyu, a Shandong native, 35 years old, formerly served as a second-rank Chinese detective in the Investigation Department of the General Patrol House. He was prosecuted by the patrol house for the armed robbery of Fang Liansheng's morphine worth 50,000 yuan. The preliminary trial acquitted Liang, but after the patrol house's lawyer, Ru Baoyi, presented sufficient reasons, the Higher Second Branch Court of Appeal sentenced him to ten years in prison. Liang was also involved with Lu A'gen and others, who have already been sentenced to death, in the kidnapping of Chen Shifan, the owner of a construction factory, at the entrance of Fuxingyuan Restaurant on Pingwang Street, Fuzhou Road, at 9:35 PM on December 19 of last year, and in the kidnapping of Li Huiqing on Guangxi Road at 1:30 AM on February 8 of this year for a large ransom. Therefore, the General Patrol House transferred Liang to the Hongkou Patrol House, and the investigating detectives Wei Jinfu and Mao Yiwen and others escorted him to the First Special District Court for interrogation. All the details have been reported in this newspaper and have now been concluded and are awaiting sentencing. Yesterday morning, Judge Xiao Xieffen presided over the sentencing in the Third Criminal Court, sentencing Liang Chengyu to death for jointly kidnapping for ransom, and to death for harboring kidnappers, to be executed.

Four Chinese Detectives Detained 118

Accused of Intimidation and Extortion

Guo Baolin, a Jiangnan native, badge number 3217 of the Xin Zha Patrol Station; Zhu Yigui, an Anhui native, badge number 1637; Zhan Yande, a Nanjing native, badge number 2869; and Long Ruilin, an Anhui native, badge number 3086, all four Chinese detectives were ordered by their captain at around 6:00 PM on the 1st of this month to cooperate with Western detectives to inspect pedestrians in their respective jurisdictions for dangerous or prohibited items. Upon returning to the patrol station at 8:00 PM after completing their duties, the captain discovered that the four Chinese detectives had engaged in intimidation and extortion while performing their official duties, and immediately ordered them to be detained separately. However, the patrol station stated that the matter was currently under investigation, so the details of the case could not be disclosed at this time. However, according to this reporter's investigation, a pedestrian named Jiang Youming passed by Baker Road and encountered the search team. The Chinese and Western detectives found Jiang suspicious and ordered him to stop for inspection. They found a lottery ticket in his possession. After obtaining evidence of a crime, the Chinese detectives resorted to extortion, ordering Jiang to pay money to be released. However, because Jiang did not have enough money to meet their demands, he was forced to take off his clothes and pawn them at a nearby pawnshop to pay the money before he was released. Afterwards, Jiang reported the incident to the Xin Zha Patrol Station, which led to the detention of the four Chinese detectives. However, whether the above account is factual remains to be determined after the patrol station's investigation is completed. At 9:30 AM yesterday, the patrol station sent the four Chinese detectives to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court, where patrol station lawyer Wang Yaotang stated that the four Chinese detectives were accused of intimidation and extortion while performing their official duties and requested that they be detained for investigation. Guo Baolin hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend him in court. Cui Yuzhen and His Wife Return to China 120

Mr. Cui Yuzhen, a Shandong native, graduated from the Economics Department of Peking University in 1926 and went to England to study currency systems and banking at the University of London for four years. He is the author of "The Theory and Practice of the Gold Standard" and "The Central Bank Theory," both of which were published by the Commercial Press. The Municipal Public Works Bureau Bans the Lujia Ferry 121

Prohibiting Docking at Wharf No. 1 of South Shanghai

To Prevent Danger to Passengers and Criminal Activity

The Municipal Public Works Bureau previously determined that the Lujia Ferry, which used small boats to tow barges, was abnormally crude. The ferry had no wharf on the Puxi side and always approached the Sixteen Pups, untied cables, and parked by sailing around the bow of the Ningshao or Sanbei Company steamer parked on Wharf No. 1 of South Shanghai, to reach the northern end of the wharf. Furthermore, because of the significant difference in height between the wharf and the ferry, the ferry operator had a barge as a walkway, with a gangplank on top, to reach the wharf. All the passengers boarded and disembarked from there, which was not only extremely dangerous, but also caused a lot of obstruction to the loading and unloading of passengers and goods on the steamer because of the large number of people and the frequent traffic. In particular, the mix of people made it easy for criminals to hide, making it extremely difficult to prevent theft. Shipping merchants have repeatedly complained and requested that the ferry be banned. The ferry was banned once in March. Then the ferry operator Gong Jisheng came to the Bureau

Page 16

and stated that the Dongmen Road Municipal Ferry Wharf would be installed soon. In fact, there was no longer any space to dock boats. He asked for a little time to find a suitable wharf to maintain his livelihood. The Bureau thought that the ferry operator's claim was not unreasonable and allowed the ferry operator to wait until the ferry wharf was installed before banning the ferry in order to consider the livelihood of the ferry operator. In July, the Dongmen Road Ferry Wharf was completed. Soon after, the dredging and repair of the floating wharf started. The Bureau immediately notified the ferry operator to stop docking at Wharf No. 1. When the floating wharf was repaired and installed, Gong Jisheng went to the Wharf and Warehouse Management Office of the Municipal Public Works Bureau and requested to continue docking. The office did not allow it. The ferry operator then docked without permission. The office detained the small boat and the ticket seller and sent them to the Water Patrol General Team for punishment, and ordered them to sign a document promising that they would no longer dock at Wharf No. 1 and would be subject to punishment if they violated the document.

A Brick Boat Accidentally Collides with an Oil Boat 125

Two Boatmen Fell into the River

The kiln cargo boat Wang Youlin was recently hired by the Zhang Yu Ji Construction Factory to load 60,000 bricks and tiles in Jiahu to transport to Shanghai for unloading at Yinxianggang. The Wang boat set off to Shanghai the other day. To make up for time, yesterday at about 3:00 AM, while sailing on the 18-mile-long Nanhuangpu River, it went the wrong way because it was dark, and crashed head-on into the Xing Hehe boat of the Shanghai Yuan Long Company, which was parked on the riverbank and carrying 300 pieces of pine oil. The bow of the Wang boat was knocked off by three or four feet, and three boatmen fell into the water. The side of the Xing boat was also broken, the oil drums were shattered, the oil was poured out, and the tide poured in, causing the boat to sink. Fortunately, it was on the riverbank and the deck was exposed. Of Wang's three crewmen, only one was rescued on the spot. It is assumed that the other two drowned. The losses suffered were great. Xing detained Wang and demanded compensation for the losses. It is said that the oil was worth more than 5,000 taels. The matter is currently being negotiated.

The British-Owned Public Bus Company 130

Announces the Dismissal of All Ticket Sellers, the Municipal Party Department and Social Bureau Intervene to Mediate

After the British-owned public bus company's ticket sellers went on strike again, the company yesterday announced the complete dismissal of the striking workers and continued to hire new workers. The Municipal Party Department and Social Bureau will discuss methods to mediate. The various situations yesterday are recorded below.

▲Traffic Situation Yesterday, the public buses in the Public Concession were still operated by ticket inspectors and newly hired workers serving as ticket sellers, barely operating Route 1 from Jing'an Temple to Laobazi Road, Route 2 from Er Yangjing Bridge to Park Bazi Square, Route 5 from Sanmaoge Bridge to North Railway Station, and Route 9 from Jing'an Temple to Tilanqiao.

The remaining routes 3, 4, 6, 7, and 10 were still out of service. The fare for Route 1 was still 20 cents across the board.

▲Request for Mediation Because of the company's tough attitude, the conditions requested by the ticket sellers were rejected. More than 150 ticket sellers have been formally dismissed by the company. Five representatives, including three unemployed workers and two employed workers, were sent to the Water and Electricity Workers' Union on the night before last to request the assistance of the Standing Director of the Union, and to the Municipal Party Department and Social Bureau to request assistance and mediation. It is reported that the Party and government organs will discuss methods to mediate. ▲The company's firmness The Public Bus Company had previously resolved at a board meeting to hire 40 new workers due to the ticket sellers' strike. They have now completed their training and are serving on the buses. Now, because the ticket sellers who had resumed work have gone on strike again, the company announced that it would continue to hire new workers starting yesterday. It is reported that the General Patrol House has hired hundreds of new workers on behalf of the company and sent them to the Connaught Road headquarters for training yesterday. The company plans to gradually restore all bus routes after the new workers have completed their training and are serving on the buses in order to maintain traffic.

▲The labor unrest is prolonged The British-owned public bus company has completely rejected the 11 conditions proposed by the strike committee. In addition to hiring new workers, yesterday it announced that all 110 ticket sellers who had re-strike would be dismissed to prevent future troubles. Therefore, the labor unrest may be difficult to resolve in a short period of time.
